| 0:13:15| I want to emphasize the recode charrette goals.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=795)|
| 0:13:20| We wanted to test the recode draft four and zoning map three at Knoxville locations.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=800)|
| 0:13:26| They were north, south, east, west, and downtown edge conditions.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=806)|
| 0:13:30| We wanted to explore how recode shapes future development and assess recode's content, format, and usability.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=810)|
| 0:13:40| The first site we looked at, you will see, is Fifth Avenue and Central Street.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=820)|
| 0:13:44| It's near where Knoxville Historic High School is located.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=824)|
| 0:13:48| The findings from the group that met, we had about six participants per group.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=828)|
| 0:13:52| We had architects, developers, and the students all spread out with each zone.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=832)|
| 0:13:56| What their comments were were that downtown edge zone is helpful for restoring density near the city core.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=836)|
| 0:14:03| There should be an overlay for potential historic structures and for recommended transit-oriented development.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=843)|
| 0:14:10| The developers of the group suggested additional parking.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=850)|
| 0:14:13| This zone allowed for on-street parking, but they thought for usable businesses that additional parking would be a great idea.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=853)|
| 0:14:21| The next study area that we looked at was in west, and it was Bearden at Homburg.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=861)|
| 0:14:27| New zones were very helpful in transitioning from lower to higher intensity uses and more walkable communities,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=867)|
| 0:14:34| but parking requirements were difficult to achieve.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=874)|
| 0:14:38| The design included street-facing, mixed-use developments of two- and three-stories| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=878)|

| 0:19:38| We found that with material restrictions, this was a challenging topic,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1178)|
| 0:19:43| because as one of our participants said, any good material can be used badly.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1183)|
| 0:19:48| Any restricted material could be used well.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1188)|
| 0:19:51| So we certainly recommend this is an area worth further study.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1191)|
| 0:19:55| Where there are material restrictions, we would recommend more specificity to the intent of the restrictions,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1195)|
| 0:20:02| perhaps including specific examples of poor usage.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1202)|
| 0:20:06| We would also recommend more specificity as to material definitions.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1206)|
| 0:20:11| For example, plastic is a fairly broad term that could be used to apply to anything from petroleum-based products to concrete to solid surface| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1211)|
| 0:20:22| or any other number of polymer-type materials.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1222)|
| 0:20:26| Design standards.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1226)|
| 0:20:28| Elements like the new chart in the code go a long way to improving usability and clarity.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1228)|
| 0:20:35| We recommend coordination of design standard language with other codes.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1235)|
| 0:20:41| For instance, references to percentage of glazing on fa√ßade should be coordinated with, or perhaps just referenced, sections of the energy code.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1241)|
| 0:20:51| There are instances where material restrictions can simply be addressed by allowable materials in the IBC fire restriction districts.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1251)|
| 0:21:01| And height limitations can be governed by the building code.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1261)|
| 0:21:05| Ensuring consistency between codes can go a long way to making the zoning ordinance easier to understand and administer.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1265)|

| 0:21:20| Words like transparency or repetition can sometimes be confusing or have multiple meanings.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1280)|
| 0:21:27| We would further recommend overall clarity of intent with regards to many of the standards.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1287)|

| 0:22:00| One area of concern is the degree to which these illustrations might start to dictate a style.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1320)|

| 0:22:29| The next recommendation is a fairly big recommendation.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1349)|
| 0:22:32| As I mentioned earlier, there were several instances, as we went through the evaluation,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1352)|
| 0:22:37| where the lack of intent made interpretation or evaluation difficult.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1357)|
| 0:22:41| We would recommend adding a section to the code that outlines the code's guiding principles when it comes to design.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1361)|
| 0:22:48| Design standards, as they currently exist in the code, outline what to do.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1368)|
| 0:22:55| They do not describe the purpose or intent of the code, the why.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1375)|
| 0:23:00| We believe that this section of guiding design principles should be the preface to all of the design standards in the document.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1380)|
| 0:23:08| What I'm illustrating here is an example of such design principles.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1388)|
| 0:23:12| These were recently developed for the city of New York City, specifically for quality, affordable housing.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1392)|
| 0:23:19| But these principles, in many ways, are universally agreed upon as good design strategies.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1399)|
| 0:23:25| Design 101, if you will.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1405)|
| 0:23:27| I'm going to highlight just a couple of these, because I think they're relevant.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1407)|
| 0:23:30| The first one is materiality.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1410)|
| 0:23:32| If you look at the bold section, a couple of these points,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1412)|
| 0:23:37| consider materials that complement rather than strictly match adjacent buildings.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1417)|
| 0:23:42| Consider using combination of materials to help articulate the facade, enhance massing, and distinguish programs at the interior.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1422)|
| 0:23:53| Consider materials with low environmental impact that are easily maintained.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1433)|
| 0:23:59| And consider the life expectancy of buildings and how materials selected will change over time.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1439)|
| 0:24:05| In many ways, the design standards aim to kind of talk to some of these principles in a what-to-do sort of fashion.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1445)|
| 0:24:14| We think it would be valuable to specifically put these principles in if these are the underlying goals.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1454)|
| 0:24:22| This next one is talking about ground floor condition.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1462)|
| 0:24:27| Consider a welcoming arrival threshold with a space designed for residents to gather.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1467)|
| 0:24:34| Consider large windows to promote visual connections between the ground floor activity and the street.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1474)|
| 0:24:39| You get the point.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1479)|
| 0:24:40| I'm not going to read through all of those.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1480)|
| 0:24:41| But overall, principles that really kind of guide why we are putting this code in place| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1481)|
| 0:24:47| and kind of govern the types of places that we want to make.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1487)|
| 0:24:54| It's important to remember that design standards and material restrictions, along with the review process, were developed for a reason.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1494)|
| 0:25:01| In essence, it's to create a floor for minimally acceptable design standard for important corridors in the city| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1501)|
| 0:25:08| and to create a review process that is manageable, transparent, and consistent.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1508)|
| 0:25:13| All of these are good things.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1513)|
| 0:25:15| However, what happens oftentimes with a prescriptive design standard is that you not only create a floor for acceptable design,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1515)|
| 0:25:24| but you also create a ceiling that could prevent outstanding design.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1524)|
| 0:25:33| The big question is, how do you safeguard the design of the city against some agreed-upon idea of bad design without limiting greatness?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1533)|
| 0:25:41| And I know we've had a data process.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1541)|
| 0:25:43| In fact, I know that given the project vision and goals, promoting greatness is the goal.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1543)|
| 0:25:48| The proposed review process outlined in the draft code would have projects subjected to design standards| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1548)|
| 0:25:55| to be reviewed by the city codes department.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1555)|
| 0:25:58| For the sake of consistency and efficiency, this process would be very prescriptive.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1558)|
| 0:26:03| It is effectively a series of checkboxes intended to be quantifiable and measurable| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1563)|
| 0:26:09| and to establish a minimum level of design standards.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1569)|
| 0:26:15| We recognize the need for this sort of kind of fast-track process,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1575)|
| 0:26:20| and with clear standards, there will be many projects for which this will work well.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=1580)|

| 1:16:21| The next one is the size limit in the office district.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4581)|
| 1:16:25| Currently, structures are limited to 10,000 square feet unless they meet certain design standards.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4585)|
| 1:16:31| Those design standards are, in my mind, pretty minimal.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4591)|
| 1:16:35| They are that the development maintains privacy of adjacent residential lots| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4595)|
| 1:16:39| through techniques such as decreased height, additional landscape and screening measures,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4599)|
| 1:16:43| building massing and design to mitigate adverse impacts of noise and lighting,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4603)|
| 1:16:47| and increased setbacks above those required from adjacent residential lots.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4607)|
| 1:16:51| Building design elements incorporate pedestrian-scale facilities such as awnings and storefront windows.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4611)|
| 1:16:57| And finally, the design of the site circulation system provides adequate and safe access| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4617)|
| 1:17:02| for both motor vehicles and alternate modes of transportation, including pedestrians and bicycles.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4622)|
| 1:17:09| There have been concerns that that size limit will make it, with design,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4629)|
| 1:17:14| if you want to go more than 10,000 square feet, that the cost of those design elements makes it infeasible.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4634)|
| 1:17:20| The purpose of the office district is, in many cases, to serve as a transition from residential areas| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4640)|
| 1:17:26| to more densely developed, intensely developed commercial areas.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4646)|
| 1:17:32| The size limit was put in to thinking that that would help achieve that goal of transition| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4652)|
| 1:17:38| from the intense commercial areas to residential areas.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4658)|
| 1:17:42| I'm sensitive to the concern of some developers that that size limit may cost them too much to exceed.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4662)|
| 1:17:52| The staff recommendation, in lieu of going back to our current standard of 30% of lots area,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4672)|
| 1:18:00| which means that on a less than two-acre parcel, you could have a 30,000-square-foot building,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4680)|
| 1:18:05| which could be next to your 1,200-square-foot home,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4685)|
| 1:18:10| is that we limit that size limit to those office districts that are but a residential,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4690)|
| 1:18:17| a single-family residential district to maintain that transition.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=4697)|

| 2:36:59| but we believe that RECODE and zoning most certainly do impact affordable housing| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=9419)|
| 2:37:05| and availability of affordable housing.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=9425)|
| 2:37:08| In basic economics 101, we learn when supply goes up while demand stays the same, prices go down.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=9428)|
| 2:37:16| Conversely, if demand goes up while supply stays the same, prices go up.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=9436)|
| 2:37:21| When it comes to housing, zoning can impact the supply and demand equation most obviously on the supply side.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=9441)|
| 2:37:28| If you've got 20 square blocks of a city for which zoning says you can only build single family homes,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=9448)|
| 2:37:34| one per block, then you get 20 housing units.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=9454)|
| 2:37:37| If you have 100 people seeking housing and only 20 housing units,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=9457)|
| 2:37:41| then prices for those housing units are going to be pushed higher.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=9461)|
| 2:37:45| So zoning can impact housing prices and affordability.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CityCouncilWSR3877190404?start=9465)|
